GRE_venizelos_assassination = {
	GRE_track_venizelos = {
		icon = GFX_decision_eng_blackshirt_march
		allowed = {
			original_tag = GRE
		}
		available = {
			has_completed_focus = GRE_venizelos_assassination_plot
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GRE_track_venizelos
				has_country_flag = GRE_preparation_in_progress
				has_country_leader = {
					character = GRE_eleftherios_venizelos
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GRE_track_venizelos
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 15
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = GRE_preparation_in_progress
		}
		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = GRE_preparation_in_progress
			custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_venizelos_assassination_plus_20_percents
			add_to_variable = {
				GRE_venizelos_plot_preparation = 20

		}

operations = {
	GRE_occupy_cyprus = {
		icon = GFX_decision_infiltrate_state
		allowed = {
			original_tag = GRE
		}
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				tag = CYP
			}
		}
		available = {
			has_war = no
			is_subject = no
			FROM = {
				has_war = no
				is_subject = no
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = ROOT
					ratio < 0.5
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				any_other_country = {
					has_guaranteed = FROM
				}
				has_active_mission = frankfurt_conference
				has_active_mission = versallies_conference
			}
		}
		visible = {
			FROM = {
				owns_state = 183
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = great_war_loser
				has_idea = idea_army_restrictions
			}
		}
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 183
			}
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 10
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			command_power > 24.9
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		complete_effect = {
			add_command_power = -25
		}
		remove_effect = {
			annex_country = {
				target = FROM
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			add_named_threat = {
				threat = 3
				name = GRE_occupy_cyprus
			}
		}
	}
}

GRE_battle_of_epirus = {
	GRE_leave_northern_epirus_mission = {
		icon = GFX_decision_infiltrate_state
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 803
			}
		}
		allowed = {
			OR = {
				tag = GRE
				tag = ITA
				tag = AUS
			}
		}
		visible = {
			OR = {
				tag = GRE
				has_country_flag = AUH_ITA_BUL_reaction_to_GRE_occupation_of_nothern_epirus
				has_country_flag = ROOT_against_GRE_occupation_of_northern_epirus
			}	
		}
		activation = {
			AUS = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject = no
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = great_war_loser
				}
				has_country_flag = AUH_ITA_BUL_reaction_to_GRE_occupation_of_nothern_epirus
			}
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = epirus_has_been_freed
			}
			803 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = GRE
			}
		}
		selectable_mission = yes
		cost = 0
		timeout_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ROOT_against_GRE_occupation_of_northern_epirus
					is_subject = no
					has_war = no
					is_subject = no
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = great_war_loser
					}
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = GRE
					type = liberate_wargoal
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = epirus_has_been_freed
			news_event = {
				id = ww1_greece.237
				days = 1
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				EPR = {
					transfer_state = 803
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ROOT_against_GRE_occupation_of_northern_epirus
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_firstbalkan.52
					days = 2
				}
				clr_country_flag = ROOT_against_GRE_occupation_of_northern_epirus
				hidden_effect = {
					remove_decision = GRE_leave_northern_epirus_mission
					remove_mission = GRE_leave_northern_epirus_mission
				}
				
			}
		}
		available = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = GRE
				}
				has_completed_focus = GRE_florence_protocol
				owns_state = 803
				else = {
					always = no
				}	
			}
			
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 15
			modifier = {
				date < 1914.1.1
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				date > 1914.2.2
				factor = 100
			}
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 400
		is_good = no
	}

					}

						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

GRE_balkan_war = {
	GRE_capture_thessaloniki = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_ignite_civil_war

		allowed = { original_tag = GRE }

		highlight_states = { highlight_state_targets = { state = 345 } }

		available = {
			345 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT } 
		}

		activation = {
			TUR = {
				owns_state = 345
				has_war_with = ROOT
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		is_good = no

		days_mission_timeout = 100

		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				TUR = { NOT = { owns_state = 345 } }
				NOT = { has_war_with = TUR }
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout GRE_capture_thessaloniki"
			add_war_support = -0.10
			add_political_power = -50
			add_stability = -0.10
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision GRE_capture_thessaloniki"
			add_war_support = 0.10
			add_political_power = 100
			add_stability = 0.10
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = GRE_high_morale
				days = 60
			}
		}
	}
}

#law legislations
GRE_reforms = {
	GRE_prohibit_child_labor = {
		icon = GFX_decision_eng_trade_unions_support
		allowed = { original_tag = GRE }
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = GRE_work_legislation
		}
		available = {
			has_country_flag = GRE_work_legislation
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = reform_in_progress
			}
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 10
        days_remove = 7
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = reform_in_progress
		}
		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = reform_in_progress
			custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_efficiency_cap_3_tt
			add_to_variable = {
				var = GRE_efficiency_cap_var
				value = 0.03
			}
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_dynamic_modifier = {
							modifier = GRE_agrarian_society_dynamic_modifier
						}
						has_dynamic_modifier = {
							modifier = GRE_balanced_approach_dynamic_modifier
						}
						has_dynamic_modifier = {
							modifier = GRE_industrializing_society_dynamic_modifier
						}
					}	
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_efficiency_cap_3_tt
				add_to_variable = {
					var = GRE_efficiency_cap_var
					value = 0.03
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {

	GRE_buy_FROM_infantry_weapons = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
		allowed = { original_tag = GRE }
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					tag = FRA
					tag = GER
					tag = ENG
					tag = AUS
				}
				
			}
		}
		available = {
			NOT = {

GRE_territorial_allegeance = {

	GRE_expand_the_front = {
		icon = GFX_decision_eng_blackshirt_march
		allowed = { original_tag = GRE }
		available = {
			original_tag = GRE
			OR = {
				any_country = {
					is_major = yes
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
				has_global_flag = great_war_ends
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GRE_is_expanding_front }
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					any_neighbor_state = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
					has_state_category = tiny_island
					has_state_category = small_island
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						state = 185
					}
					ROOT = {
						owns_state = 758
						owns_state = 826
					}
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			original_tag = GRE
			has_completed_focus = GRE_expand_the_front2
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = GRE_force_the_king_to_abdicate
				has_country_flag = great_war_loser
			}
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = FROM.OWNER
			}
		}
		
		days_re_enable = 20
		days_remove = 40
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 500
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				check_variable = { GRE_number_of_states_transfered > 3 }
			}
			# remove epistratoi first
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = {
					NOT = {
						state = 182
						state = 185
						state = 731
						state = 758
						state = 826
					}
				}
				OR = {
					has_idea = gre_epistratoi
					has_idea = gre_epistratoi2
					has_idea = gre_epistratoi3
				}
			}
		}
		state_target = yes
		
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = GRE
					is_claimed_by = GRE
				}
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = GRM
				OR = {
					any_neighbor_state = {
						CONTROLLER = {
							OR = {
								AND = {
									original_tag = GRE
									NOT = { tag = GRE }
								}
								is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							}
							
						}
					}
					state = 900 #IM SPECIAL
				}
				NOT = { state = 898 }
			}
		}
		cost = GRE_expansion_cost?20
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = GRE_is_expanding_front
			add_to_variable = { GRE_expansion_cost = 20 }
		}
		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = GRE_is_expanding_front
			FROM = { transfer_state_to = ROOT }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment
				amount = -300
				producer = GRE
			}
			add_to_variable = { GRE_number_of_states_transfered = 1 }
		}
	}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = gre_epistratoi3
				}
				remove_ideas = gre_epistratoi3
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = gre_epistratoi2
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = gre_epistratoi2
					add_idea = gre_epistratoi3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = gre_epistratoi
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = gre_epistratoi
					add_idea = gre_epistratoi2
				}
			}
		}
	}

			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = gre_monarchist_garrison_control_none
			trigger = {
				has_completed_focus = GRE_commit_to_neutrality
				898 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 1 compare = equals } }
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = gre_monarchist_garrison_control_weak
			trigger = {
				has_completed_focus = GRE_commit_to_neutrality
				898 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 2 compare = equals } }
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = gre_monarchist_garrison_control_strong
			trigger = {
				has_completed_focus = GRE_commit_to_neutrality
				898 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 3 compare = equals } }
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = gre_monarchist_garrison_control_total
			trigger = {
				has_completed_focus = GRE_commit_to_neutrality
				898 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 4 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
			}
		}
		available = {
			has_full_control_of_state = 898
			has_civil_war = no
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_commit_to_neutrality }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = GRE_expand_influence_monarchists_trigger_tt
					898 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = GRE_expand_influence_venizelists_trigger_tt
					898 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 4 compare = less_than } }
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GRE_already_expanding_influence_flag }
		}
		highlight_states = { highlight_state_targets = { state = 898 }  }
		on_map_mode = map_only
		cost = 898.GRE_garrison_control_cost?10
		days_remove = 14
		fire_only_once = no
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = battle_of_influence
			898 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
		}
		cancel_if_not_visible = yes
		complete_effect = { set_country_flag = GRE_already_expanding_influence_flag }
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente }
				898 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_expand_influence_venizelists_tt
					hidden_effect = {
						if = {
							limit = { check_variable = { GRE_garrison_control < 4 } }
							add_to_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 1 }
							ROOT = { add_to_variable = { var = GRE_venizelist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
							ROOT = { subtract_from_variable = { var = GRE_monarchist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						}
					}
					GRE_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					GRE_garrison_control_cost_calculation_venizelists = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_commit_to_neutrality }
				898 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_expand_influence_monarchists_tt
					hidden_effect = {
						subtract_from_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 1 }
						ROOT = { subtract_from_variable = { var = GRE_venizelist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						ROOT = { add_to_variable = { var = GRE_monarchist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
					}
					GRE_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					GRE_garrison_control_cost_calculation_monarchists = yes
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = GRE_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 110
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente
				898 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente
				898 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 3 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				factor = 5
			}
		}
	}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = battle_of_influence
			803 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
		}
		cancel_if_not_visible = yes
		complete_effect = { set_country_flag = GRE_already_expanding_influence_flag }
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente }
				803 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_expand_influence_venizelists_tt
					hidden_effect = {
						if = {
							limit = { check_variable = { GRE_garrison_control < 4 } }
							add_to_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 1 }
							ROOT = { add_to_variable = { var = GRE_venizelist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
							ROOT = { subtract_from_variable = { var = GRE_monarchist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						}
					}
					GRE_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					GRE_garrison_control_cost_calculation_venizelists = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_commit_to_neutrality }
				803 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_expand_influence_monarchists_tt
					hidden_effect = {
						subtract_from_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 1 }
						ROOT = { subtract_from_variable = { var = GRE_venizelist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						ROOT = { add_to_variable = { var = GRE_monarchist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
					}
					GRE_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					GRE_garrison_control_cost_calculation_monarchists = yes
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = GRE_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 110
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente
				803 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente
				803 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 3 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				factor = 5
			}
		}
	}

			has_civil_war = no

				limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_commit_to_neutrality }

					tooltip = GRE_expand_influence_monarchists_trigger_tt

				limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = GRE_expand_influence_venizelists_trigger_tt
					757 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 4 compare = less_than } }
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GRE_already_expanding_influence_flag }
		}
		highlight_states = { highlight_state_targets = { state = 757 }  }
		on_map_mode = map_only
		cost = 757.GRE_garrison_control_cost?10
		days_remove = 14
		fire_only_once = no

			has_country_flag = battle_of_influence

							limit = { check_variable = { GRE_garrison_control < 4 } }

							ROOT = { add_to_variable = { var = GRE_venizelist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
							ROOT = { subtract_from_variable = { var = GRE_monarchist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						}
					}
					GRE_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					GRE_garrison_control_cost_calculation_venizelists = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_commit_to_neutrality }
				757 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_expand_influence_monarchists_tt
					hidden_effect = {
						subtract_from_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 1 }
						ROOT = { subtract_from_variable = { var = GRE_venizelist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						ROOT = { add_to_variable = { var = GRE_monarchist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
					}
					GRE_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					GRE_garrison_control_cost_calculation_monarchists = yes
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = GRE_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 110
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente

					NOT = { has_state_flag = GRE_venizelist_state_flag }
				}
			}

			}
		}

			key = gre_monarchist_garrison_control_strong2
			trigger = {
				has_country_flag = battle_of_influence_royalist_side
				975 = {
					check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 3 compare = equals }
					has_state_flag = GRE_venizelist_state_flag

		}
		icon = {
			key = gre_monarchist_garrison_control_total
			trigger = {
				has_country_flag = battle_of_influence_royalist_side
				975 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 4 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
			}
		}
		available = {
			has_full_control_of_state = 975
			has_civil_war = no
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_commit_to_neutrality }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = GRE_expand_influence_monarchists_trigger_tt
					975 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = GRE_expand_influence_venizelists_trigger_tt
					975 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 4 compare = less_than } }
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GRE_already_expanding_influence_flag }
		}
		highlight_states = { highlight_state_targets = { state = 975 }  }
		on_map_mode = map_only
		cost = 975.GRE_garrison_control_cost?10
		days_remove = 14
		fire_only_once = no
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = battle_of_influence
			975 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
		}
		cancel_if_not_visible = yes
		complete_effect = { set_country_flag = GRE_already_expanding_influence_flag }
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente }
				975 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_expand_influence_venizelists_tt
					hidden_effect = {
						if = {
							limit = { check_variable = { GRE_garrison_control < 4 } }
							add_to_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 1 }
							ROOT = { add_to_variable = { var = GRE_venizelist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
							ROOT = { subtract_from_variable = { var = GRE_monarchist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						}
					}
					GRE_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					GRE_garrison_control_cost_calculation_venizelists = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_commit_to_neutrality }
				975 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_expand_influence_monarchists_tt
					hidden_effect = {
						subtract_from_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 1 }
						ROOT = { subtract_from_variable = { var = GRE_venizelist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						ROOT = { add_to_variable = { var = GRE_monarchist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
					}
					GRE_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					GRE_garrison_control_cost_calculation_monarchists = yes
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = GRE_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 110
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente
				975 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente
				975 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 3 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				factor = 5
			}
		}
	}

			trigger = {
				has_country_flag = battle_of_influence_royalist_side
				899 = {
					check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 2 compare = equals }
					has_state_flag = GRE_venizelist_state_flag
				}
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = gre_monarchist_garrison_control_strong
			trigger = {
				has_country_flag = battle_of_influence_royalist_side
				899 = {
					check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 3 compare = equals }
					NOT = { has_state_flag = GRE_venizelist_state_flag }
				}
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = gre_monarchist_garrison_control_strong2
			trigger = {
				has_country_flag = battle_of_influence_royalist_side
				899 = {
					check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 3 compare = equals }
					has_state_flag = GRE_venizelist_state_flag
				}
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = gre_monarchist_garrison_control_total
			trigger = {
				has_country_flag = battle_of_influence_royalist_side
				899 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 4 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
			}
		}
		available = {
			has_full_control_of_state = 899
			has_civil_war = no
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_commit_to_neutrality }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = GRE_expand_influence_monarchists_trigger_tt
					899 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = GRE_expand_influence_venizelists_trigger_tt
					899 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 4 compare = less_than } }
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GRE_already_expanding_influence_flag }
		}
		highlight_states = { highlight_state_targets = { state = 899 }  }
		on_map_mode = map_only
		cost = 899.GRE_garrison_control_cost?10
		days_remove = 14
		fire_only_once = no
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = battle_of_influence
			899 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
		}
		cancel_if_not_visible = yes
		complete_effect = { set_country_flag = GRE_already_expanding_influence_flag }
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente }
				899 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_expand_influence_venizelists_tt
					hidden_effect = {
						if = {
							limit = { check_variable = { GRE_garrison_control < 4 } }
							add_to_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 1 }
							ROOT = { add_to_variable = { var = GRE_venizelist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
							ROOT = { subtract_from_variable = { var = GRE_monarchist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						}
					}
					GRE_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					GRE_garrison_control_cost_calculation_venizelists = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_commit_to_neutrality }
				899 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_expand_influence_monarchists_tt
					hidden_effect = {
						subtract_from_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 1 }
						ROOT = { subtract_from_variable = { var = GRE_venizelist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						ROOT = { add_to_variable = { var = GRE_monarchist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
					}
					GRE_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					GRE_garrison_control_cost_calculation_monarchists = yes
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = GRE_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 110
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente
				899 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente
				899 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 3 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				factor = 5
			}
		}
	}

					custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_expand_influence_monarchists_tt
					hidden_effect = {
						subtract_from_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 1 }
						ROOT = { subtract_from_variable = { var = GRE_venizelist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						ROOT = { add_to_variable = { var = GRE_monarchist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
					}
					GRE_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					GRE_garrison_control_cost_calculation_monarchists = yes
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = GRE_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 110
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente
				1018 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente
				1018 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 3 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				factor = 5
			}
		}

					tooltip = GRE_expand_influence_venizelists_trigger_tt
					861 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 4 compare = less_than } }
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GRE_already_expanding_influence_flag }
		}

							limit = { check_variable = { GRE_garrison_control < 4 } }

							ROOT = { add_to_variable = { var = GRE_venizelist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
							ROOT = { subtract_from_variable = { var = GRE_monarchist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						}
					}

					custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_expand_influence_monarchists_tt
					hidden_effect = {
						subtract_from_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 1 }

						ROOT = { add_to_variable = { var = GRE_monarchist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
					}
					GRE_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					GRE_garrison_control_cost_calculation_monarchists = yes
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = GRE_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 110
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente
				861 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }

				has_country_flag = battle_of_influence_royalist_side
				342 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 1 compare = equals } }
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = gre_monarchist_garrison_control_weak
			trigger = {
				has_country_flag = battle_of_influence_royalist_side
				342 = {
					check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 2 compare = equals }
					NOT = { has_state_flag = GRE_venizelist_state_flag }
				}
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = gre_monarchist_garrison_control_weak2
			trigger = {
				has_country_flag = battle_of_influence_royalist_side
				342 = {
					check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 2 compare = equals }
					has_state_flag = GRE_venizelist_state_flag
				}
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = gre_monarchist_garrison_control_strong
			trigger = {
				has_country_flag = battle_of_influence_royalist_side
				342 = {
					check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 3 compare = equals }
					NOT = { has_state_flag = GRE_venizelist_state_flag }
				}
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = gre_monarchist_garrison_control_strong2
			trigger = {
				has_country_flag = battle_of_influence_royalist_side
				342 = {
					check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 3 compare = equals }
					has_state_flag = GRE_venizelist_state_flag
				}
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = gre_monarchist_garrison_control_total
			trigger = {
				has_country_flag = battle_of_influence_royalist_side
				342 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 4 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
			}
		}
		available = {
			has_full_control_of_state = 342
			has_civil_war = no
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_commit_to_neutrality }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = GRE_expand_influence_monarchists_trigger_tt
					342 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = GRE_expand_influence_venizelists_trigger_tt
					342 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 4 compare = less_than } }
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GRE_already_expanding_influence_flag }
		}
		highlight_states = { highlight_state_targets = { state = 342 }  }
		on_map_mode = map_only
		cost = 342.GRE_garrison_control_cost?10
		days_remove = 14
		fire_only_once = no
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = battle_of_influence
			342 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
		}
		cancel_if_not_visible = yes
		complete_effect = { set_country_flag = GRE_already_expanding_influence_flag }
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente }
				342 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_expand_influence_venizelists_tt
					hidden_effect = {
						if = {
							limit = { check_variable = { GRE_garrison_control < 4 } }
							add_to_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 1 }
							ROOT = { add_to_variable = { var = GRE_venizelist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
							ROOT = { subtract_from_variable = { var = GRE_monarchist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						}
					}
					GRE_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					GRE_garrison_control_cost_calculation_venizelists = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_commit_to_neutrality }
				342 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_expand_influence_monarchists_tt
					hidden_effect = {
						subtract_from_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 1 }
						ROOT = { subtract_from_variable = { var = GRE_venizelist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						ROOT = { add_to_variable = { var = GRE_monarchist_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
					}
					GRE_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					GRE_garrison_control_cost_calculation_monarchists = yes
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = GRE_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 110
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente
				342 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente
				342 = { check_variable = { var = GRE_garrison_control value = 3 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				factor = 5
			}
		}
	}

crisis = {
	GRE_retreat_from_new_territories = {
		icon = GFX_decision_eng_blackshirt_march
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 345
				state = 731
				state = 184
			}
		}
		allowed = {
			OR = {
				tag = GRE
				tag = FRA
			}
		}
		activation = {
			has_country_flag = GRE_FRA_expansion_of_macedonian_front
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = has_retreated_from_new_territories
				has_global_flag = great_war_ends
				has_war_with = GER
				has_war_with = FRA
			}
			is_subject = no
			any_state = {
				has_state_flag = french_salonika
				OR = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = GRE
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = FRA
				}
			}
			OR = {
				345 = {
					OR = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = GRE
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = FRA
					}
				}
				731 = {
					OR = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = GRE
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = FRA
					}
				}
				184 = {
					OR = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = GRE
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = FRA
					}
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_war_with = GER
				has_war_with = FRA
				is_subject = yes
				has_global_flag = great_war_ends
			}
		}
		available = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				divisions_in_state = { state = 345 size < 1 }
				divisions_in_state = { state = 731 size < 1 }
				divisions_in_state = { state = 184 size < 1 }
			}
			else = { always = yes }
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = has_retreated_from_new_territories
			731 = {
				set_border_war = yes
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_support_to_entente }
				GRE = { give_military_access = FRA }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_country = { clr_country_flag = GRE_FRA_expansion_of_macedonian_front }
				GRE = {
					country_event = {
						id = ww1_greece.46
						days = 26
					}
				}
			}
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GRE_FRA_expansion_of_macedonian_front
					is_subject = no
					NOT = { tag = GRE }
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = GRE
					type = puppet_wargoal_focus
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				GRE = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_completed_focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente
						}
						uncomplete_national_focus = {
							focus = GRE_negotiations_with_entente
							uncomplete_children = yes
							refund_political_power = no
						}
						unlock_national_focus = GRE_commit_to_neutrality
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_war_with = FRA }
						GER = { add_to_faction = PREV }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 100
		is_good = no
	}
}

	}

	GRE_trigger_pontic_revolt = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_civil_support
        allowed = {
            original_tag = GRE
        }
        visible = {
            has_country_flag = pontus_rebellion
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = pontic_revolt_done
			}
        }
		available = {
			any_state = {
				is_core_of = PON
				has_dynamic_modifier =  { 
					modifier = GRE_pontic_nationalism
				}
			}
		}
        days_remove = 2
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 50
		}
        remove_effect = {
			set_country_flag = pontic_revolt_done
			PON = {
				division_template = {
					name = "Pontic Brigades"
					regiments = {
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					}
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = PON
					has_dynamic_modifier =  { 
						modifier = GRE_pontic_nationalism
					}
				}
				CONTROLLER = {
					country_event = {
						id = ww1_greece.185
						days = 1
					}
					release = PON
				}
				transfer_state_to = PON
				add_core_of = PON
				create_unit = { 
					division = "name = \"Pontic Brigades\" division_template = \"Pontic Brigades\" start_experience_factor = 0.5" 
					owner = PON
				}
